int Fibonacci(int n){
	if ( n == 0 )
		return 0;
	else if ( n == 1 )
		return 1;
	else

int find_maximum(int a[], int n) {
	int c, max, index;
	
	max = a[0];
	index = 0;
	
	for (c = 1; c < n; c++) {
		if (a[c] > max) {
		index = c;
		max = a[c];
		}
	}

	return index;
}

int add_digits(int n) {
	static int sum = 0;
	
	if (n == 0) {
		return 0;
	}	
	sum = n%10 + add_digits(n/10);

	return sum;
}

void print_floyd(int n) {
	static int row = 1, c = 1;
	int d;
	
	if (n <= 0)
		return;
	
	for (d = 1; d <= row; ++d)
		printf("%d ", c++);
	
	printf("\n");
	row++;
	
	print_floyd(--n);   
}

int find_minimum(int a[], int n) {
	int c, min, index;
	
	min = a[0];
	index = 0;
	
	for (c = 1; c < n; c++) {
		if (a[c] < min) {
			index = c;
			min = a[c];
		}
	}
	
	return index;
}

INFO  ConsoleInput:68 - Founded only a function
INFO  ConsoleInput:71 - Function: 
void bubble_sort(long list[], long n){
	long c, d, t;
	
	for (c = 0 ; c < ( n - 1 ); c++){
		for (d = 0 ; d < n - c - 1; d++){
			if (list[d] > list[d+1]){
				t         = list[d];
				list[d]   = list[d+1];
				list[d+1] = t;
			}
		}
	}
}

void concatenate(char p[], char q[]) {
	int c, d;
	c = 0;
	
	while (p[c] != '\0') {
		c++;  	
	}
	
	d = 0;
	
	while (q[d] != '\0') {
		p[c] = q[d];
		d++;
		c++;	
	}
	
	p[c] = '\0';
}

void reverse2(char *x, int begin, int end){
	char c;
	
	if (begin >= end)
		return;
	
	c          = *(x+begin);
	*(x+begin) = *(x+end);
	*(x+end)   = c;
	
	reverse2(x, ++begin, --end);
}

	while(*first==*second){
		if ( *first == '\0' || *second == '\0' )
			break;

		second++;

	if ( a >= 'A' && a <= 'Z' )
		a = a + 'a' - 'A';
	
	if ( a == 'a' || a == 'e' || a == 'i' || a == 'o' || a == 'u')
		return 1;
	
	return 0;
}

INFO  ConsoleInput:64 - Function: \check_subsequence(char[],char[])
INFO  ConsoleInput:68 - Founded only a function
INFO  ConsoleInput:71 - Function: 
int check_subsequence (char a[], char b[]) {
	int c, d;
	
	c = 0;
	d = 0;
	
	while (a[c] != '\0') {
		while ((a[c] != b[d]) && b[d] != '\0') {
			d++;
		}
		if (b[d] == '\0')
			break;
		d++;
		c++;
	}
	if (a[c] == '\0')
		return 1;
	else
		return 0;
}

void find_frequency(char s[], int count[]) {
	int c = 0;
	
	while (s[c] != '\0') {
		if (s[c] >= 'a' && s[c] <= 'z' ) 
		count[s[c]-'a']++;
		c++;
	}
}

void bsort (int * table, int l){
	int i, temp, nb;
	char fini;
	fini = 0;
	nb = 0;
	while ( fini==0 && (nb < l-1)){    
		fini = 1;
		for (i=0 ; i<l-1 ; i++)         
			if (table[i] < table[i+1]){   
				fini = 0;
				temp = table[i];
				table[i] = table[i + 1];
				table[i + 1] = temp;
			}
			nb++;
		}
}

void reverse_array(int *pointer, int n){
	int *s, c, d;
	
	s = (int*)malloc(sizeof(int)*n);
	
	if( s == NULL )
		exit(EXIT_FAILURE);
	d = 0 ;
	for ( c = n - 1; c >= 0 ; c-- ){
		*(s+d) = *(pointer+c);
		d++;
	}
	
	for ( c = 0 ; c < n ; c++ )
		*(pointer+c) = *(s+c);
	
	free(s);
}

int check_anagram(char a[], char b[]){
	int first[26], second[26], c = 0;
	first[20] = 0;
	second[26]=0;
	while (a[c] != '\0'){
		first[a[c]-'a']++;
		c++;
	}
	
	c = 0;
	
	while (b[c] != '\0'){
		second[b[c]-'a']++;
		c++;
	}
	
	for (c = 0; c < 26; c++){
		if (first[c] != second[c])
		return 0;
	}
	
	return 1;
}

int Tritype(int i, int j, int k){
	int trityp = 0;
	if (i < 0 || j < 0 || k < 0)    
		return 3;
	if (i + j <= k || j + k <= i || k + i <= j)
		return 3;    
	if (i == j) 
		trityp = trityp + 1;           
	if (i == k) 
		trityp = trityp + 1;           
	if (j == k) 
		trityp = trityp + 1;           
	if (trityp >= 2)                          
		trityp = 2;
	return trityp;
}

void Merge1(int t1[3], int t2[3], int t3[6]) {
	int i = 0, j = 0, k = 0 ;
	while (i < 3 && j < 3) {
		if (t1[i] < t2[j]) {   
			t3[k] = t1[i];
			i++;
		}else {
			t3[k] = t2[j];
			j++;
		}
		k++ ;
	}
	while (i < 3) {      
		t3[k] = t1[i];
		i++;
		k++;
	}
	while (j < 3) {        
		t3[k] = t2[j];
		j++;
		k++;
	}
}

	int i, k=0;
	
	for(i=0; i<2; i++) {   
		if(a[i] == 0)

	if(a[i] != a[i+1])

		return 0;

			k++;
	}
	return 1;

int Bsearch( int A[10], int x) {
	int low, high, mid, found ;
	
	low = 0 ;
	high = 9 ;
	found = 0 ;
	while( high > low ){ 
		mid = (low + high) / 2 ;
		
		if( x == A[mid] )                
			found = 1;
		
		if( x > A[mid] )                   
			low = mid + 1 ;
		else
			high = mid - 1;
	}  
	mid = (low + high) / 2 ;
	
	if( ( found != 1)  && ( x >= A[mid]) )
		found = 1; 
	
	return found ;
}

int ArrayCmp(int n, unsigned char* t1, unsigned char* t2) {
	int i;
	for (i = 0; i < n; i++) { 
		if (t1[i] > t2[i])        
			return -1;
	else if (t1[i] < t2[i])    
		return 1;
	}
	return 0;
}

void bsort (int * table, int l){
	int i, temp, nb;
	char fini;
	fini = 0;
	nb = 0;
	while ( fini==0 && (nb < l-1)){    
		fini = 1;
		for (i=0 ; i<l-1 ; i++)         
			if (table[i] < table[i+1]){   
				fini = 0;
				temp = table[i];
				table[i] = table[i + 1];
				table[i + 1] = temp;
			}
			nb++;
		}
}
